<h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства_2"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:know.html>know</a></strong> (<i>third-person <a href = vnd.unilang:singular.html>singular</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:know.html>knows</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:know.html>knowing</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:know.html>knew</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:know.html>known</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:colloquial.html>colloquial</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> nonstandard</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:know.html>knew</a></b>)
</p>
